The nose behind this fragrance is Alberto Morillas. Top notes are Calabrian bergamot, Water Notes, Grapefruit and Fig Leaf; middle notes are Ambroxan, Black Pepper, Patchouli, Violet Leaf and Papyrus; base notes are Incense, Musk, Tonka Bean and Saffron. </p><div v-pre class='fragrantica-blockquote'><p>In late July 2016, Versace launches Dylan Blue, a new fragrance from the Versace Pour Homme collection under the license of Euroitalia, which includes the original from 2008 and the Oud Noir edition from 2013.</p>

<p>Its aromatic, woody - fougere composition with fresh aquatic notes, Calabrian bergamot, grapefruit and fig leaves at the top, develops with a heart of violet leaf, papyrus wood, organic patchouli, black pepper and ambrox. Mineral musks, tonka bean, incense and saffron wrap the composition up and give it a fougere vibe.</p>

<p>The advertising campaign, which was shot by Bruce Weber, includes models Gigi Hadid, Trevor Signorino, Alan Jouban, Louis Solywoda and Filip Sjunnesson, as well as martial arts athletes Nic Thompson, Travis Conover, Adam von Rothfelder, Lukasz Grabowski and Levi Morgan.</p>

<p>The bottle with clean lines comes in dark, Mediterranean blue with a golden cap and a golden Medusa seal. The fragrance is available as a 30, 50, 100 and 200 ml ml Eau de Toilette with an additional after shave lotion, deodorant and bath &amp; shower gel.</p></div><p class="reviewstrigger" padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2175270">AverageVersaceUser</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-10-18">10/18/24 16:02</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>7.9 / 10 - Good Scent<br />
<br />
Over the last few months this has been my signature scent and I have really enjoyed it however there some things I don't like about it. <br />
<br />
First off the opening is a very citrusy blast but don't be fooled it doesn't smell ANYTHING like eros as some may think, it's quite synthetic and so some may not enjoy it. That being said the drydown is way better, it's more musky and ambery keeping it fresh yet sweet.<br />
<br />
It lasts pretty long around 5 to 6 hours which is great for a blue fragrance!<br />
<br />
The projection is also pretty good with around 2 to 3 feet for the first 2.5 hours and after that may become more of a skin scent. <br />
<br />
I would recommend this for all year and it's great as a first scent! <br />
<br />
But remember test before you buy!</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="2320154"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=2320154#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2319175" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.88);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; I find it very linear through its short lifespan.  It smells a bit like Lynx Bergamot and Pink Pepper - which is one of my least favourite Lynx scents - but more smoky, probably from the incense and saffron.  The watery/violet leaf notes are there but very faint.<br />

Performance for me is very moderate, needing at least 6 sprays and then a top up every 3 hours or so.  I’m glad I didn’t pay &gt;A$100.<br />

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2281442" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="A_serious_reviewer"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2252602"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/himg/o.69247.png" class="comments-avatar"alt="A_serious_reviewer" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2281442ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck0x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2281442" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(250,247,236,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2252602">A_serious_reviewer</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-13">09/13/24 08:23</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>== Notes == <br />
Present but not intensive grapefruit and slight aquatic top notes combined with an intensive violet middle note laying on a robust and complex musky peppery earthy foundation mainly made of musk, ambroxan, incense, papyrus, fig leaf and tonka. <br />
<br />
<br />
== Mood ==<br />
profound - deep - strong - masculine - calming - old interior - marine - sensual - attractive - seductive <br />
<br />
<br />
== Concept == <br />
The Dylan Blue follows Versace's mantra, almost unique in the industry, which consists in associating in a well-balanced and original manner strong citrus and flowery accords. This cologne can be seen as a deep/night blue type of fragrance, however is not an equivalent of Dior Sauvage, Bleu de Channel or even any Aqua di Gio. It stands as a unique concept, unique fragrance. <br />
<br />
<br />
== When to wear ==<br />
late afternoon - evening - night<br />
spring and summer<br />
excellent for a date<br />
good for dinner at the restaurant or any outside activities at night<br />
not an office fragrance<br />
<br />
<br />
== Why to buy ==<br />
unique in terms of notes and notes association<br />
cheap for the quality<br />
performant, long lasting, good sillage<br />
well-balanced <br />
no other equivalent or clone in other brands<br />
deep and attractive/seductive while calming<br />
very nice smelling overally</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="2281442"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=2281442#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2281284" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.84);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1197425">LavenderMilk</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-09-03">09/03/24 14:13</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is my opinion as a woman who won't wear this. However, maybe what I say will be useful.<br />
<br />
This is a good perfume.<br />
<br />
This is a perfectly good perfume of the "hey, honey, just but me something good" kind - for somebody who doesn't really care what they wear, they just want it to be decent. Who wears one perfume they have until it's out, and then picks almost anything and does the same. But if they wear such perfumes as this, it's a great choice. And it's not in the "really expensive" bracket, it's just a bit more expensive than truly cheap perfumes.<br />
<br />
It's a "many man" perfume, bit it's not obnoxious, or old-fashioned, it's noticeable, but it smells office-safe. Is indeed similar to many other perfumes, bit it's a good solid version of that cold-ish marine-ish smell with a sprinkle of bergamot and woods. (Don't overspray it, for god's sake, find the golden mean of probably 2-4 spritzes.)<br />
<br />
I can't say how long it lasts, sorry. It's probably not a 10+ hours beast.<br />
<br />
D&amp;G One to me is in the same vein, although that one is absolutely different in composition, it's a spicy woody: a safe office frag for almost anyone. And I love that Karl Lagerfeld Grey thingie, which is more similar. It's like an every day blazer which goes with almost everything, it's not "interesting" because it's the weather's job to be interesting.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; Heard a ton of buzz about this one and decided to test it. Went around the store with a strip of this, a strip of Prada Luna Rossa Ocean, and a strip of AdG Pour Homme. I asked about 15 people (mostly women) which they thought would be best on me for a summer scent. The votes were about even for this and AdG, but AdG had a lot of caveats - "It's something my ex would wear" "All the guys at the bar wear this" "It smells plain". So I picked Dylan Blue.<br />
<br />
I LOVE the way this smells. It's really masculine without having any "old man" smells, it's fresh, a little spicy, and don't even get me started on the patchouli. There's nothing crazy or unique about this scent, but in my opinion this is the best in quality and in price among its competitors. Women enjoy it, men enjoy it, and most importantly, I enjoy it. Will absolutely be purchasing a second bottle.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="2255487"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=2255487#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2254751" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(250,249,251,0.75);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; While I understand why many people enjoy this fragrance, it didn't resonate with me. I was hoping for a more blue, fresh, and aquatic scent, but the dominant incense note overshadowed those elements.<br />
<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2211782">Pavel_russia</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-03">08/03/24 12:50</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Это очень яркий и выраженный аромат. Раскрывается с цитрусовыми и морскими нотами и амброксаном. Дальше на первый план выходит терпкая сладость и свежесть с амброксаном. Амброксан с чем-то ещё, может это фиалка, чувствуется на протяжении всего ношения. Сладость довольно выражена. Чувствуется ладан. Как по мне, не подходит для регулярного ношения. Подходит для вечеринок, встреч с девушкой или друзьями, для похода в гости. Можно одеть и на работу, но не на всякую, надо соотвествующе выглядеть, желательно быть в полуклассике или просто хоршей качественной не сильно вольной одежде. Для меня это довольно интимный аромат, он черезчур резкий и сладкий для меня, поэтому я бы не хотел показывать его всем, но при этом он не отталкивает, я бы поставил ему 4 из 5.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2180598">Cadester34</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-08-02">08/02/24 13:10</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Was looking for a cheaper alternative to my BDC edt and I think I found it. $60 for a 100 ml bottle is hard to beat. When people said this smells like shower gel they weren’t lying. It has a super fresh opening which would be perfect for beach wear or warm days. In my opinion BDC beats this in the opening with the heavy grapefruit note where Dylan Blue leans more towards the aquatic notes with hints of citrus. Still a super pleasant scent, I’m just a sucker for those citrus notes. The dry down is where Dylan Blue excels BDC for me. BDC edt really fades away after the first hour and becomes a  skin scent. Dylan Blue maintains much better silage and longevity through the heat. The scent of the dry down is awesome as well. Still maintains that fresh scent but also opens up with hints of musk, woods, and spice. I asked family to choose their favorite of BDC and Dylan Blue and it was hard for most because they smelled practically identical. Overall probably the best value blue fragrance you can purchase. Although Dylan Blue will probably be my daily in the heat now, BDC will still hold a place in my heart for those special occasions.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1678076">EpicFragrances</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-26">07/26/24 20:27</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This was my first blue fragrance and I love it, It has this shower gel vibe with some sort of darkness to it. I've gotten some compliment here and there, in my opinion this surpasses the more popular blue fragrances like sauvage or BDC. This is one of the only fragrances that I can wear anywhere anytime without hesitation and I won't offend anyone because this has a very mass appealing DNA. The quality you're getting for the price you're paying is amazing (discounters of course), plus the performance of this great for an EDT concentration. Definitely pick it up as your first blue fragrance.<br />
<br />
Smell: 8.5/10<br />
Longevity: 8 hours<br />
Projection: Medium to Strong<br />
Price: $50-$55 for 100ml at discounters</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="2230555"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=2230555#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2230515" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.82);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:4,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:&quot;male_unisex&quot;,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="4"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc2222466" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Cosmos_PMF"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108424"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.2108424.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Cosmos_PMF" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Xerjoff/Torino22-77059.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.77059.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Torino22"title="Torino22"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma2222466ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck2x3"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd2222466" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.76); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/2108424">Cosmos_PMF</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-07-18">07/18/24 11:41</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>This is THE dumb reach simple smooth blue shower gel fragrance.<br />
<br />
The scent profile is very popular in itself, fresh out the shower, mass appealing, typical blue fragrance with a very smooth twist, most age groups but probably more suited for teenagers. <br />
To my nose it's very similar to the Dior Sauvage DNA  (edp mostly) rather than other blue fragrances. <br />
Ambroxan based, watery and citrusy fragrance with an incense undertone. <br />
<br />
I've heard there was a reformulation before, on my skin it lasts 4-6hrs with soft to moderate projection, I overspray it usually. <br />
<br />
In versatility this is in the top, day and night all seasons apart from very cold weather, use it as a daily signature easily. <br />
<br />
The bottle is pretty cute, the cap is annoying because you gotta hold the bottle while carrying it to not risk dropping it off your toes while holding its cap (it happened to me) <br />
<br />
It does the job for you to smell good and it brings compliments to the right audience, niche lovers will not enjoy this scent (plot twist, im the niche lover). <br />
PS: Compliments will vary, you would get girls sniffing you saying you smell clean and masculine or you get the "u smell like my ex" card. <br />
<br />
Not sure if I could call it overrated or underrated tho<br />
<br />
Last note, I always see the comparison between this and YSL Y edp but I don't understand it, they are very different even though both of them are classified as blue fragrances. I own both, I prefer YSL Y edp as a daily long lasting sharp greener signature and Dylan blue as a smoother more popular DNA.<br />
<br />
Versace pour homme Dylan Blue: shower gel, gets compliments but you won't feel unique wearing this for sure. 8/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="2222466"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=2222466#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent2222356" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.9);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:0,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:null}"></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Descriptions are accurate, it's a blue summer cologne, but probably is best used in a somewhat formal and dressed up way. Unique scent, as the amber added makes it more versatile than just a fresh fragrance. But the fact that this fragrance is so popular, for what? Good, but overhyped. I asked for the price, and they said 130 of my nations currency, which is around 90 american dollars. I was genunely confused, especially for a Eau De Toilette, to be this much. This was a huge love for me early on in my collection. Is this still a daily-wear after all the new fragrances I have discovered?<br />
I see Dylan Blue continues to sell, &amp; it sells a lot. Immediately I can tell you it's worth the hype, but especially for a starter collection. <br />
<br />
First off, this is beyond worth the discounter price. It's versatile (all season), has a pleasing opening (amber citruses with a shower gel dry down) and lasts damn-near forever. My friend wore this on our 2 hour walk in the blazing heat and for the whole walk the scent just projected off him and beamed into my nose. (he put it on much earlier as well)<br />
<br />
Next, you will find it for like $50CAD for the 100ml, amazing value.<br />
<br />
Lastly, it's a crowd-pleaser, definitely in the same category as Sauvage with its performance &amp; versatility.<br />
<br />
It's hated because you get compliments too easily from it.<br />

Although it might be interesting from a cost-benefit perspective for someone looking for one of the most popular blue fragrances, for me, this is one of Morillas's least inspired works.<br />
<br />
The opening is heavy on aquatic notes that, if not actual calone, certainly resemble it. The incense is barely noticeable. The dry down is lighter and more balanced, with a base of ambroxan, which I like, but it has zero incense and ends up being quite generic. So, DB really sits in a very safe middle ground between Sauvage EDT and BDC. I prefer scents that are a bit bolder and don't rely solely on the ambroxan + citrus combo to be pleasant, such as Sauvage EDP in contrast to the EDT.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; This was my first signature scent and will forever hold a place in my collection. Very safe blind buy for beginners, as with most Versace fragrances.<br />
<br />
The best way to describe this fragrance would be to call it a combination of Dior Sauvage and Bleu de Chanel EDT, made a bit sweeter and with a hint of incense smokiness.<br />
<br />
Longevity with my 2023 batch is 6-8 hours with strong projection for the first 2-3 hours. 4-6 sprays and everyone within a few feet can smell you. It lasts a few days on clothes. <br />
<br />
I have moved away from this price range but this scent never disappoints when I do decide to wear it.<br />
<br />

padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/1928180">FWJPG</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2024-05-22">05/22/24 16:37</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>Got my first bottle last year(50ml) after seeing it hyped up like, everywhere. I was quite pleased with the smell since I had just  started my collection at the time, Dylan Blue being my second purchase😅. 1 year and 18 frags later, I can say that this thing macerated a bit, since I was busy with other recent purchases and coming back to it made me think that even tho I still have almost half a bottle of it, I should order a backup bottle, so I ordered a 100ml size bottle. <br />
<br />
This should answer the question "Do I like it?" and of course the answer is Yes without a doubt. It is a bit overhyped imo but nonetheless, quite unique among the ocean of the blue fragrances that already exist. <br />
<br />
Should you buy it? Definitely yes, it is a no brainer frag that you could easily pull out for any occasion making it your signature if you want to. I am not sure about the performances on recent batches, the current bottle that I have is from 2023 if I remember correctly and it performs alright that meaning 6-7 hours with a good projection in first 2 to 3 hours than it becomes moderate to skin scent when it approaches the 7 hours mark. For an EDT, I am quite impressed, since is so refreshing and out of the shower type of scent. Ofc I've heard a lot of stories about the first batches that lasted 24 hours and so on, but recent reformulations are ok imo and be sure I will give an update on the 100 ml bottle too. Hope that helped if you were in doubts, just don't get very high expectations from it, easy to blind buy but I recommend to try it before buying it tho as it can be a bit overwhelming for some.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; <br />
the hate on Bleu when it first came out has nothing on hate for this<br />
<br />
the hate on Sauvage when it first came out (and is still on going) has nothing when it comes to hate on this<br />
<br />
this fragrance will be hated on for a long time to come, its like that with almost every mass marketed new fragrance from a big designer house now a days <br />
<br />
i think people expect way too much from designers now a days, and some can deliver here and there, but we must realize that days of unique designer fragrances are long gone. almost every new release from now on will be a mass appeal "money grab" fragrance <br />
<br />
all of the houses are doing it, why should one house design a very unique fragrance that aficionados will appreciate while their competitors can make a synthetic fragrance that will sell by the millions and get all the $.. especially if it is a big global designer house that has profit in mind, and not a small niche house thats trying to please a few thousand people.. <br />
<br />
this "mass appeal" fragrance is going to be a new trend and "old school" noses expecting something unique will have a very hard time accepting it.. people would want a niche type of a new fragrance to be released for around $80 by a designer house, and than they would be happy.. although that has happened in the past, very rarely, those days are long gone..<br />
<br />
i went to dillards a few days ago just to try to see what this new Versace is about.. the store rep sprayed it on a tester strip.. a few seconds later a girl that was standing about 3 meters away said "o my god what is that, that smells good".. immediately i got a lot of ambroxane and Dior Sauvage type of fragrance from this.. monster silage and longevity, as I was walking out of dillards i was carrying a small paper strip with me, and i heard another woman walking behind me say how "someone here smells good".. <br />
<br />
so there you have it.. its a "compliment whore" type of fragrance.. if art is what you are after, please pass.. if compliments and pleasing others, and receiving attention is what you are after, go buy this! <br />
<br />
yesterday i went to sephora to get a small sample of this to test on my skin.. took the sample to work today, and all my female coworkers loved it.. they said it smells great.. <br />
<br />
if you want ladies attention this is for you.. if you expected a lot from Versace, a natural and unique fragrance, this is not for you.. <br />
<br />
this was meant to be a competitor to Sauvage.. they have a similar vibe.. its not a great fragrance, but its a fragrance that has its purpose, and it does that purpose amazingly well !</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; I just find myself reaching for these more than others. <br />
<br />
It's like that shirt that you think is your favorite shirt (because you probably spent too much on it) but really, the shirt you wear all the time and feel the most comfortable and cool in is your favorite---this is the latter.<br />
<br />
If you're looking for an easy-reach that projects and lasts and won't murder your wallet, you've come to the right place. It's aquatic, but not too much, sweet, but not too much, and the ambroxan pushes off the skin in a satisying way (this stuff pops).<br />
<br />
As others have said, no one ever says, "You smell basic" in real life. You either smell good or you don't. Dylan Blue will make you smell good.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="2062346"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=2062346#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent1122102" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(255,253,234,0.74);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:1,&quot;spring&quot;:1,&quot;summer&quot;:1,&quot;autumn&quot;:1,&quot;day&quot;:1,&quot;night&quot;:1,&quot;longevity&quot;:3,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Back bone the Ambroxan, though  synthetic, is better rounded and blend as compared to CDS. Incense and Black pepper provide perfect spiciness and darkness, a little over shadowing Aquatic notes. Tonka and Musk give the scent power to stay and a little mature vibe too.<br />
Develops well on skin with moderate silage and good longevity. Very versatile ,massive crowd pleaser , definitely not for connoisseur noses, but just keep in mind how common these noses are?<br />
Perfect all season all occasion Fresh Aromatic frag. Just imagine CDS despite enjoying higher applaud, had to bring out 3 flankers while this very only one is doing well , still.<br />
To me it loses to BDC Parfum by a nick and a little better than Dior Sauvage.<br />
Attention to Medusa and fine designing on golden cap with extremely Cool Cobalt Blue bottle make the presentation quite elaborate and a look at the bottle gives a perfect insight into what the product is about.<br />
A very well done scent by Versace an 8.5/10 for me.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="1122102"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=1122102#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent832926" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(248,249,236,0.89);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:5,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:4,&quot;sillage&quot;:2,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="5"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; Bottle from - 2016<br />
<br />
Dylan Blue is a nice,fresh,clean,pleasant,sexy scent and at the same time,courtesy to a incense note,he is a little bit dark as well.Nevertheless it is a beautiful and well-blended fragrance.<br />
<br />
Longevity - 7/10(7+hours)<br />
Silage/projection -7/10((nice projection for the first 2-3 hours,silage also exist)<br />
Weather - all time(Versatility-9/10) <br />
Age - 19+ <br />
Compliments - 9/10<br />
Scent - 8/10<br />
<br />
Main notes according to me -<br />
ambroxan,bergamot,grapefruit,pepper,water notes,incense.<br />
<br />
The drydown is nice and i get some - <br />
tonka bean,incense,ambroxan and patchouli.<br />
<br />
Emotions -sexy,date,fun,modern,fresh,relax,casual.<br />
<br />
Reminds me a little bit of Dior Sauvage,Acqua di Gio Profumo and Bleu de Chanel.Perfect for more less any ocasion and any time of year.Ladies love this scent.<br />
Could be a nice signature scent.If you want a huge compliment getter,you can't go wrong with it.</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="832926"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=832926#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="40031" sentiment="positive"></reviews-infinity>

padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc825390" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Lmuradian"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/879102"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.879102.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Lmuradian" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma825390ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck5x1"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd825390" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(247,244,242,0.79); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/879102">Lmuradian</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-05-23">05/23/17 16:39</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>I originally went to purchase a birthday present for my cousin. And i knew i was going to purchase this exact fragrance. At first i was attacked by the female sales associates at Macys with a "This is Azzaro Wanted &amp; Mr.Burberry"  i told them i'm not interested in these scents. I made my way to where Dylan Blue was placed sniffed it to make sure this was worth a full retail purchase and it definitely was. I ended up purchasing a gift set for myself as well. I have been wearing it continuously here in Los Angeles in the high late spring/summer heat. I've been complimented so many times on this fragrance in the past two weeks more than a lot of the fragrances i own. you get a big blast of citruses up top which is nice but very strong ,This scent shines 15 minutes in and stays shining through out the duration of this fragrance which i get 8-10 hours the sillage disappears right around the 7 hour mark. But the scent of the dry down is amazing. Does it remind me of Sauvage and or BDC? Its in the same genre but it is its own scent which is very good. Nothing super groundbreaking but it has a lot of personality and sex appeal to it.This will become a mens classic in the many years to come.<br />
<br />
<br />
Scent: 9/10<br />
Sillage: 8/10<br />
Longevity: 9/10<br />
Compliment Factor: 9/10</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="825390"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=825390#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div><div id="parent894418" class="cell fragrance-review-box" style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72);" itemprop="review" itemtype="http://schema.org/Review" itemscope><div style="display: flex;flex-wrap: wrap;justify-content: end;position: relative"><user-perfume-votes :perfume-votes="{&quot;rating&quot;:2,&quot;winter&quot;:0,&quot;spring&quot;:0,&quot;summer&quot;:0,&quot;autumn&quot;:0,&quot;day&quot;:0,&quot;night&quot;:0,&quot;longevity&quot;:0,&quot;sillage&quot;:0,&quot;gender&quot;:null,&quot;relation&quot;:&quot;have&quot;}"><div itemprop="reviewRating" itemtype="http://schema.org/Rating" itemscope><meta itemprop="ratingValue" content="2"/><meta itemprop="bestRating" content="5"/></div></user-perfume-votes></div><div class="grid-x" style="width 100%; padding-top: 0.4rem; padding-bottom: 0.4rem;"><div id="cc894418" class="cell small-2" sticky-container><div v-sticky><div class="comments-avatar" style="position: relative;" itemprop="author" itemtype="http://schema.org/Person" itemscope><meta itemprop="name" content="Ryanmmas26"/><span class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/761961"><img loading="lazy" itemprop="image" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/avatari/m.761961.jpg" class="comments-avatar"alt="Ryanmmas26" style="opacity: 0.85;"></span><div class="perfume-wearing-avatar"><span class="idLinkify" title="/perfume/Armaf/Club-de-Nuit-Precieux-93272.html"><img loading="lazy" src="https://fimgs.net/mdimg/perfume/mm.93272.jpg"class="perfume-wearing-icon" alt="Club de Nuit Precieux"title="Club de Nuit Precieux"></span></div><div class="karma-avatar-new"><div id="karma894418ckNxM" class="ckNxM ck4x2"></div></div></div></div></div><div id="dd894418" class="cell small-10 flex-container flex-dir-column"sticky-container><div class="flex-child-shrink" v-sticky style="background: rgba(249,249,243,0.72); padding: 0.2rem;"><p><b class="idLinkify" title="https://www.fragrantica.com/member/761961">Ryanmmas26</b><span class="vote-button-legend" style="padding: 0 1rem;" itemprop="datePublished" content="2017-12-28">12/28/17 15:04</span></p></div><div class="flex-child-auto" style="position: relative;"><div v-pre itemprop="reviewBody"><p>First initial review —-<br />
<br />
Not going to lie I was very let down from this fragrance and I didn’t really have high expectations for this in the start.<br />
<br />
This starts off smelling like a typical fruity,sweet frag that has been typical of a lot of the newer releases but it quickly transitions into a sharp,aromatic freshie that to my nose was very synthetic and actually cheap smelling. To my nose this smelled like it could have been a scent from AXE. <br />
<br />
I didn’t completely hate this as I did enjoy the bergamot and violet in this scent as it did have a nice aromatic nature but there was some screechy note that made it sharp,synthetic and off putting. To be honest it kind of smelled like dirty pool water.lol<br />
<br />
My girlfriend did not like this and it was sad because I got Dylan Blue and Mont Blanc Legend intense and she hated Dylan blue but loved Legend intense.lol<br />
<br />
Performance— This was a strong suit as it was a very good projector and has good Sillage as it lasted 8 hours as well.<br />
<br />
Overall rating— 5.5 out of 10 ! Not the worst but I would pick so many even cheaper frags over Dylan Blue (even from the house of Versace I like Blue Jeans way better than Dylan Blue)</p></div></div><div class="flex-child-shrink"><div style="display:flex; align-items: baseline;"><vote-buttons initial_status="neutral" item_id="40031"comment_id="894418"vote_for="perfumeReview"></vote-buttons><share path="/perfume/Versace/Versace-Pour-Homme-Dylan-Blue-40031.html?ccid=894418#focus-zone"></share></div></div></div></div></div>                            <reviews-infinity :random-colors="[&quot;#fefcee&quot;,&quot;#faf7ec&quot;,&quot;#f9f9f3&quot;,&quot;#f8f9ec&quot;,&quot;#fffdea&quot;,&quot;#faf9fb&quot;,&quot;#faf5f2&quot;,&quot;#f7f4f2&quot;]" :perfume-id="40031" sentiment="negative"></reviews-infinity>
